\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{etpwm\+Action\+Qual\+\_\+t}{etpwmActionQual\_t}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{etpwm_8h_af381c9819d1969fe0a1b617ad2bf5a13}{etpwm\+Action\+Qual\+\_\+t}}}



Enumeration to define the pulse width modulation (E\+T\+P\+WM) action qualifiers.
